107 7.2 Time W ork ed e x ample 2 
 C onv er t 3.7 hour s into hour s and minutes . 
 3.7 hour s = 
 3 whole hour s + 0.7 o f an hour 
 Either 
 0.7 327 60 = 42 
 Ther e ar e 60 minutes in 1 hour so ther e ar e 
 0.7 327 60 minutes in 0.7 o f an hour . 
 Or 
 7 327 6 = 42 
 0.1 ( one tenth) o f an hour equals 6 minutes , 
 so 0.7 (se v en tenths) o f an hour 
 equals 7 327 6 minutes .

223 16.1 The law s o f arithme tic Which is corr ec t ? 
 C an y ou r emember the rules 
 f or calculations with dif f er ent 
 oper ations ? 
 In S tage 5, y ou learned ho w the f our oper ations , addition, 
 sub tr ac tion, multiplication and division f ollo w 
 a par ticular or der . 
 In this unit , y ou will learn ho w br ack e ts can be used to change 
 the or der o f oper ations . 16.1 The law s o f arithme tic W e ar e going to 205 225 use the law s o f arithme 
 tic to simplif y calculations 225 under s tand the or der o f oper ations and use br ack e ts to change 
 the or der o f oper ations . 
 A rule tells y ou what y ou can and can 222 t do . 
 In mathematics , y ou mus t f ollo w the rule 
 to do multiplication and division be f or e 
 addition and sub tr ac tion. associativ e rule br ack e ts commutativ e rule dis tributiv e rule or der o f oper ations 3 + 7 327 4 = 40 (3 + 7) 327 4 = 40

224 Arun and Mar cus ar e calculating using the number s 5, 6 and 7. Arun writes 5 + 6 327 7 = 47 Ho w can Mar cus write his calculation ? 
 In this sec tion, y ou will learn ho w to help Mar cus write his calculation. I w ant to multiply 
 6 and 7 and add my 
 r esult to 5. I w ant to add 5 and 6 
 and then multiply b y 7. W ork ed e x ample 1 
 Why do these calculations giv e dif f er ent ans w er s ? 
 A 3 327 4 + 6 B 3 327 (4 + 6) In calculation A w e do the multiplication 
 f i rst : 3 327 4 + 6 = 12 + 6 = 18 In calculation B w e do the oper ation in 
 br ack e ts fir s t : 3 327 (4 + 6) = 3 327 10 036 = 30 The or der o f oper ations is: 
 Br ack e ts 
 Multiplication and division 
 Addition and sub tr ac tion 
 The number s and oper ations ar e 
 the same, but the br ack e ts identif y the 
 oper ation that is done fir s t . 
 Ans w er : The calculations giv e dif f er ent ans w er s because the br ack e ts 
 in B change the or der in which oper ations ar e done.

 r eflect a squar e in a mirr or line, if you choose 
 
 one corner of the new squar e then it will ha v e the 
 
 same x-coor dinate or y-coor dinate as one corner of the 
 old squar e. It isn 222t possible to r eflect a squar e wher e all 
 the corner s of the r eflected squar e ha v e completely

 y ou ho w inter es ting Mathematics can be and mak e y ou w ant to e xplor e and inv es tigate

 Mathematics is e v er ywher e. De v eloping our skills in mathematics mak es us be t ter
